# Description
 Arb,avax,ftm,op chain have the same on-chain activity.They are all 352 days in chain.<br />The cluster interacted same Dapp.<br />![image.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2024/png/1534364/1716776003188-b83eb12c-ed80-4e48-b134-c413c6fbcd0e.png#averageHue=%23151526&clientId=udf467665-3b08-4&from=paste&height=786&id=uff817fd5&originHeight=786&originWidth=1813&originalType=binary&ratio=1&rotation=0&showTitle=false&size=514978&status=done&style=none&taskId=u31093cea-60f6-4854-9d58-0b315d38387&title=&width=1813)<br />The addresses of the cluster consistent interaction behavior in layerzero transations.<br />The interaction of No Protocol Name,Abracadabramoney,Angle,Stargate,CoreDAO,Harmonybridge,Radiantcapital have same source and destination.More importantly amount and timeline are consistent.
